A reusable dialog/popup component.\n// Closes when pressing Escape or clicking the overlay background.\n//\n// Usage:\n//   <Modal isOpen={showModal} onClose={() => setShowModal(false)} title=\"Create Goal\">\n//     <form>...</form>\n//   </Modal>\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport default function Modal({ isOpen, onClose, title, children, size = 'md' }) {\n  // Close modal when user presses Escape key\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const handleEsc = (e) => {\n      if (e.key === 'Escape') onClose()\n    }\n    if (isOpen) {\n      document.addEventListener('keydown', handleEsc)\n      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden' // prevent background scrolling\n    }\n    return () => {\n      document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleEsc)\n      document.body.style.overflow = ''\n    }\n  }, [isOpen, onClose])\n\n  if (!isOpen) return null\n\n  // Size variants\n  const sizeClasses = {\n    sm: 'max-w-md',\n    md: 'max-w-lg',\n    lg: 'max-w-2xl',\n    xl: 'max-w-4xl',\n  }\n\n  return (\n    // Dark overlay background\n    <div className=\"fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4\">\n      <div\n        className=\"absolute inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50\"\n        onClick={onClose} // clicking outside closes modal\n      />\n\n      {/* Modal Box */}\n      <div className={`relative bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-xl w-full ${sizeClasses[size]} max-h-[90vh] flex flex-col`}>\n        {/* Header */}\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200\">\n          <h3 className=\"text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900\">{title}</h3>\n          <button\n            onClick={onClose}\n            className=\"p-1.5 rounded-lg text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors\"\n          >\n            <X size={20} />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Scrollable Content */}\n        <div className=\"overflow-y-auto flex-1 p-6\">\n          {children}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"

1)}\n          disabled={currentPage === 0}\n          className=\"p-2 rounded-lg border border-gray-300 text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors\"\n        >\n          <ChevronLeft size={16} />\n        </button>\n\n        {/* Page number buttons */}\n        {Array.from({ length: Math.min(totalPages, 5) }, (_, i) => {\n          // Show pages around the current page\n          let page = i\n          if (totalPages > 5) {\n            if (currentPage < 3) page = i\n            else if (currentPage > totalPages - 3) page = totalPages - 5 + i\n            else page = currentPage - 2 + i\n          }\n          return (\n            <button\n              key={page}\n              onClick={() => onPageChange(page)}\n              className={`w-9 h-9 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-colors ${\n                page === currentPage\n                  ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white'\n                  : 'border border-gray-300 text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50'\n              }`}\n            >\n              {page + 1}\n            </button>\n          )\n        })}\n\n        <button\n          onClick={() => onPageChange(currentPage + 1)}\n          disabled={currentPage >= totalPages - 1}\n          className=\"p-2 rounded-lg border border-gray-300 text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors\"\n        >\n          <ChevronRight size={16} />\n        </button>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"

\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// This component guards pages that require authentication.\n// If the user is NOT logged in \u2192 redirect to /login\n// If roles are specified and user doesn't have the right role \u2192 redirect to /dashboard\n//\n// Usage:\n//   <ProtectedRoute>                    \u2192 requires login\n//   <ProtectedRoute roles={['ADMIN']}>  \u2192 requires ADMIN role\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport default function ProtectedRoute({ children, roles = [] }) {\n  const { user, loading } = useAuth()\n\n  // While checking saved login (from localStorage), show nothing\n  if (loading) {\n    return (\n      <div className=\"min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-50\">\n        <div className=\"animate-spin rounded-full h-12 w-12 border-b-2 border-blue-600\" />\n      </div>\n    )\n  }\n\n  // Not logged in \u2192 go to login page\n  if (!user) {\n    return <Navigate to=\"/login\" replace />\n  }\n\n  // Logged in but wrong role \u2192 go to dashboard\n  if (roles.length > 0 && !roles.includes(user.role)) {\n    return <Navigate to=\"/dashboard\" replace />\n  }\n\n  // All checks passed \u2192 render the page\n  return children\n}\n"

\u2502\n//   \u2502          \u2502   (children)         \u2502\n//                   "type": "file",
                  "path": "frontend2\\src\\context\\AuthContext.jsx",
                  "content": "import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react'\nimport authService from '../services/authService'\nimport toast from 'react-hot-toast'\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 AUTH CONTEXT \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// This is like a \"global variable\" that stores the logged-in user's info.\n// Any component in the app can access who's logged in using useAuth() hook.\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n// Step 1: Create the context (empty container)\nconst AuthContext = createContext(null)\n\n// Step 2: Create the Provider (wraps the whole app and provides the data)\nexport function AuthProvider({ children }) {\n  // State: current logged-in user (or null if not logged in)\n  const [user, setUser] = useState(null)\n  // State: whether we're still checking if user is logged in\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n\n  // When the app starts, check if there's already a saved login session\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const savedUser = localStorage.getItem('user')\n    const savedToken = localStorage.getItem('token')\n\n    if (savedUser && savedToken) {\n      try {\n        setUser(JSON.parse(savedUser))\n      } catch {\n        // If the saved data is corrupted, clear it\n        localStorage.removeItem('user')\n        localStorage.removeItem('token')\n      }\n    }\n    setLoading(false)\n  }, [])\n\n  /**\n   * Login function\n   * - Calls the auth API\n   * - Saves token + user to localStorage (persists across browser refresh)\n   * - Updates the user state\n   */\n  const login = async (email, password) => {\n    try {\n      const data = await authService.login(email, password)\n\n      // The API returns: { token, userId, name, email, role, department, managerId }\n      const userData = {\n        userId: data.userId,\n        name: data.name,\n        email: data.email,\n        role: data.role,       // \"ADMIN\" | \"MANAGER\" | \"EMPLOYEE\"\n        department: data.department,\n        managerId: data.managerId,\n      }\n\n      // Save to localStorage so user stays logged in after page refresh\n      localStorage.setItem('token', data.token)\n      localStorage.setItem('user', JSON.stringify(userData))\n\n      setUser(userData)\n      toast.success(`Welcome back, ${userData.name}!`)\n      return userData\n    } catch (error) {\n      const message = error.response?.data?.msg || 'Login failed. Please check your credentials.'\n      toast.error(message)\n      throw error\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Logout function\n   * - Calls the logout API\n   * - Clears localStorage\n   * - Resets user state\n   */\n  const logout = async () => {\n    try {\n      await authService.logout()\n    } finally {\n      setUser(null)\n      toast.success('Logged out successfully')\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Helper functions to check the user's role (makes code more readable)\n  const isAdmin = () => user?.role === 'ADMIN'\n  const isManager = () => user?.role === 'MANAGER'\n  const isEmployee = () => user?.role === 'EMPLOYEE'\n  const isAdminOrManager = () => user?.role === 'ADMIN' || user?.role === 'MANAGER'\n\n  // The value object: everything we want to share with the whole app\n  const value = {\n    user,\n    login,\n    logout,\n    loading,\n    isAdmin,\n    isManager,\n    isEmployee,\n    isAdminOrManager,\n  }\n\n  return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>\n}\n\n// Step 3: Custom hook so components can easily access auth data\n// Usage: const { user, login, logout, isAdmin } = useAuth()\nexport function useAuth() {\n  const context = useContext(AuthContext)\n  if (!context) {\n    throw new Error('useAuth must be used inside <AuthProvider>. Check your App.jsx.')\n  }\n  return context\n}\n"
                },
                {
                  "name": "NotificationContext.jsx",
                  "type": "file",
                  "path": "frontend2\\src\\context\\NotificationContext.jsx",
                  "content": "import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react'\nimport notificationService from '../services/notificationService'\nimport { useAuth } from './AuthContext'\nimport toast from 'react-hot-toast'\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 NOTIFICATION CONTEXT \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Manages real-time notifications using SSE (Server-Sent Events).\n// SSE = the server continuously pushes updates to us (like a one-way WebSocket).\n// When a manager approves your goal, you instantly get a notification!\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nconst NotificationContext = createContext(null)\n\nexport function NotificationProvider({ children }) {\n  // List of notifications loaded from the server\n  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState([])\n  // Count of unread notifications (shown as a badge on the bell icon)\n  const [unreadCount, setUnreadCount] = useState(0)\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)\n\n  const { user } = useAuth()\n  // ref to keep track of the SSE connection (so we can close it on logout)\n  const eventSourceRef = useRef(null)\n\n  // Load initial notifications when user logs in\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (user) {\n      loadNotifications()\n      startSSEStream()\n    } else {\n      // User logged out: close SSE connection and clear notifications\n      stopSSEStream()\n      setNotifications([])\n      setUnreadCount(0)\n    }\n\n    // Cleanup: close SSE when component unmounts\n    return () => stopSSEStream()\n  }, [user])\n\n  // Load notifications from the REST API\n  const loadNotifications = async () => {\n    try {\n      setLoading(true)\n      const data = await notificationService.getNotifications(0, 50)\n      // The API returns paginated data: { content: [...], totalElements, ... }\n      const notifList = data?.content || data || []\n      setNotifications(notifList)\n      // Count how many are unread\n      setUnreadCount(notifList.filter((n) => n.status === 'UNREAD').length)\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Failed to load notifications:', error)\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Start SSE connection for real-time updates\n  const startSSEStream = () => {\n    stopSSEStream() // close any existing connection first\n\n    const token = localStorage.getItem('token')\n    if (!token) return\n\n    try {\n      eventSourceRef.current = notificationService.subscribeToStream(\n        // On new notification received:\n        (newNotification) => {\n          setNotifications((prev) => [newNotification, ...prev])\n          setUnreadCount((prev) => prev + 1)\n          // Show a toast popup for important notifications\n          if (newNotification.priority === 'HIGH' || newNotification.actionRequired) {\n            toast(newNotification.message, { icon: '\ud83d\udd14' })\n          }\n        },\n        // On error:\n        (err) => {\n          console.warn('SSE error, will retry...', err)\n        }\n      )\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to start SSE stream:', err)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Stop SSE connection\n  const stopSSEStream = () => {\n    if (eventSourceRef.current) {\n      eventSourceRef.current.close()\n      eventSourceRef.current = null\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Mark a single notification as read\n  const markAsRead = async (notifId) => {\n    try {\n      await notificationService.markAsRead(notifId)\n      setNotifications((prev) =>\n        prev.map((n) =>\n          n.notificationId === notifId ? { ...n, status: 'READ' } : n\n        )\n      )\n      setUnreadCount((prev) => Math.max(0, prev - 1))\n    } catch (error) {\n      toast.error('Failed to mark notification as read')\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Mark all notifications as read\n  const markAllAsRead = async () => {\n    try {\n      await notificationService.markAllAsRead()\n      setNotifications((prev) => prev.map((n) => ({ ...n, status: 'READ' })))\n      setUnreadCount(0)\n      toast.success('All notifications marked as read')\n    } catch (error) {\n      toast.error('Failed to mark all as read')\n    }\n  }\n\n  const value = {\n    notifications,\n    unreadCount,\n    loading,\n    loadNotifications,\n    markAsRead,\n    markAllAsRead,\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <NotificationContext.Provider value={value}>\n      {children}\n    </NotificationContext.Provider>\n  )\n}\n\n// Custom hook to use notifications anywhere in the app\n// Usage: const { notifications, unreadCount, markAsRead } = useNotifications()\nexport function useNotifications() {\n  const context = useContext(NotificationContext)\n  if (!context) {\n    throw new Error('useNotifications must be used inside <NotificationProvider>')\n  }\n  return context\n}\n"
                }

          { bg: 'bg-red-50',   border: 'border-red-100',   dot: 'bg-red-500',   emoji: '\u274c' },\n  GOAL_COMPLETION_REQUEST:   { bg: 'bg-blue-50',  border: 'border-blue-100',  dot: 'bg-blue-500', \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport default function ProfilePage() {\n  const { user } = useAuth()\n\n  const [passwordForm, setPasswordForm] = useState({\n    currentPassword: '',\n    newPassword: '',\n    confirmPassword: '',\n  })\n  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)\n  const [showPasswords, setShowPasswords] = useState(false)\n  const [passwordChanged, setPasswordChanged] = useState(false)\n\n  const fields are required')\n      return\n    }\n    if (passwordForm.newPassword !== passwordForm.confirmPassword) {\n      toast.error('New passwords do not match')\n      return\n    }\n    if (passwordForm.newPassword.length < 6) {\n      toast.error('New password must be at least 6 characters')\n      return\n    }\n    if (passwordForm.newPassword === passwordForm.currentPassword) {\n      toast.error('New password must be different from your current password')\n      return\n    }\n\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await currentPassword: '', newPassword: '', confirmPassword: '' })\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Failed to change password. Check your current password.')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Role descriptions for fresher understanding\n  const roleDescriptions = {\n    ADMIN: 'Full access: </div>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Info rows */}\n          <div className=\"grid gap-4\">\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-gray-50              <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-800 font-medium\">{user?.email}</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl\">\n              <Building size={18} className=\"text-gray-400 flex-shrink-0\" />\n              <div>\n                <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-500 font-medium\">Department</p>\n                <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-800 font-medium\">{user?.department || 'Not assigned'}</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"flex items-center font-medium\">Your Role</p>\n                <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-800 font-medium\">{user?.role}</p>\n                <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-500 mt-0.5\">{roleDescriptions[user?.role]}</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl\">\n              <User size={18} className=\"text-gray-400 flex-shrink-0\" />\n              <div>\n                <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-500 font-medium\">User ID</p>\n                <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-800 font-mono\">#{user?.userId}</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Change Password Card */}\n        <div className=\"card\">\n '../../components/common/StatusBadge'\nimport { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext'\nimport { reviewCycleService } from '../../services/reviewService'\nimport toast from 'react-hot-toast'\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 REVIEW CYCLES PAGE \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// /api/v1/review-cycles/active\n// default function ReviewCyclesPage() {\n  const { isAdmin } = useAuth()\n\n  const [cycles, setCycles] = useState([])\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false)\n  const [editCycle, setEditCycle] = useState(null)\n  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)\n\n  const [form, setForm] = useState({\n    title: '',\n    startDate: '',\n    endDate: '',\n    requiresCompletionApproval: true,\n    evidenceRequired: true,\n  })\n\n  useEffect(() => { loadCycles() }, [])\n\n  const loadCycles = async () => {\n    setLoading(true)\n    try {\n      const data = await reviewCycleService.getAllCycles()\n      setCycles(data?.content || data || [])\n    } catch {\n      toast.error('Failed to load review cycles')\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const openCreate = () => {\n    setEditCycle(null)\n    setForm({ title: '', startDate: '', endDate: '', requiresCompletionApproval: true, evidenceRequired: true })\n    setShowModal(true)\n  }\n\n  const openEdit = (cycle) => {\n    setEditCycle(cycle)\n    setForm({\n      title: cycle.title,\n      startDate: cycle.startDate,\n      endDate: cycle.endDate,\n      requiresCompletionApproval: cycle.requiresCompletionApproval,\n      evidenceRequired: cycle.evidenceRequired,\n    })\n    setShowModal(true)\n  }\n\n  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    if (!form.title || !form.startDate || !form.endDate) {\n      toast.error('Title, start date, and end date are required')\n      return\n    }\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      if (editCycle) {\n        await reviewCycleService.updateCycle(editCycle.cycleId, form, editCycle.status)\n        toast.success('Review cycle updated!')\n      } else {\n        await reviewCycleService.createCycle(form)\n        toast.success('Review cycle created!')\n      }\n      setShowModal(false)\n      loadCycles()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Operation failed')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <Layout title=\"Review Cycles\">\n      <div className=\"flex justify-between items-center mb-6\">\n        <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-500\">\n          Manage performance review periods. Create cycles to trigger employee self-assessments.\n        </p>\n        {isAdmin() && (\n          <button onClick={openCreate} className=\"btn-primary flex items-center gap-2\">\n            <Plus size={18} /> New Cycle\n          </button>\n        )}\n      </div>\n\n      {loading ? (\n        <LoadingSpinner />\n      ) : cycles.length === 0 ? (\n        <div className=\"card text-center py-16\">\n          <RefreshCw size={48} className=\"mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300\" />\n          <p className=\"text-gray-500\">No review cycles created yet</p>\n          {isAdmin() && (\n            <button onClick={openCreate} className=\"btn-primary mt-4\">Create First Cycle</button>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      ) : (\n        <div className=\"grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3\">\n          {cycles.map((cycle) => (\n            <div key={cycle.cycleId} className=\"card hover:shadow-md transition-shadow\">\n              <div className=\"flex items-start justify-between mb-3\">\n                <StatusBadge status={cycle.status || 'UPCOMING'} />\n                {isAdmin() && (\n                  <button onClick={() => openEdit(cycle)}\n                    className=\"text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 p-1\">\n                    <Edit2 size={16} />\n                  </button>\n                )}\n              </div>\n              <h3 className=\"font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-2\">{cycle.title}</h3>\n              <div className=\"space-y-1.5 text-sm text-gray-600\">\n                <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n                  <Calendar size={14} className=\"text-gray-400\" />\n                  <span>{cycle.startDate} \u2192 {cycle.endDate}</span>\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"flex gap-3 mt-3\">\n                  <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${cycle.requiresCompletionApproval ? 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700' : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-500'}`}>\n                    {cycle.requiresCompletionApproval ? 'Approval Required' : 'No Approval'}\n                  </span>\n                  <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${cycle.evidenceRequired ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-500'}`}>\n                    {cycle.evidenceRequired ? 'Evidence Required' : 'No Evidence'}\n                  </span>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Create/Edit Modal */}\n      <Modal isOpen={showModal} onClose={() => setShowModal(false)}\n        title={editCycle ? '\u2014'}</p>\n          {subtitle && <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1\">{subtitle}</p>}\n        </div>\n        <div className={`w-12 h-12 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center ${color.replace('text-', 'bg-').replace('-600', '-100')}`}>\n          <Icon size={24} className={color} />\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n\nexport default function EmployeeDashboard() {\n  const { user } = useAuth()\n  const navigate = useNavigate()\n\n  const [metrics, setMetrics]           = useState(null)\n  const [recentGoals, setRecentGoals]   = useState([])\n  const [pendingReviews, setPendingReviews] = useState([])\n  const [loading, setLoading]           = useState(true)\n  const [error, setError]               = useState(null)\n\n  useEffect(() => { loadData() }, [])\n\n  const loadData = async () => {\n    setLoading(true)\n    setError(null)\n    try {\n      const [metricsRes, goalsRes, reviewsRes] = await Promise.allSettled([\n        reportService.getDashboardMetrics(),\n        goalService.getGoals(0, 8),\n        performanceReviewService.getReviews(0, 10),\n      ])\n      if (metricsRes.status === 'fulfilled') setMetrics(metricsRes.value)\n      if (goalsRes.status === 'fulfilled') {\n        const list = goalsRes.value?.content || goalsRes.value || []\n        setRecentGoals(list)\n      }\n      if (reviewsRes.status === 'fulfilled') {\n        const list = reviewsRes.value?.content || reviewsRes.value || []\n        setPendingReviews(list.filter(r => r.status === 'PENDING' || r.status === 'MANAGER_REVIEW_COMPLETED'))\n      }\n    } catch {\n      setError('Failed to load dashboard data.')\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (loading) return <Layout title=\"My Dashboard\"><LoadingSpinner message=\"Loading dashboard...\" /></Layout>\n\n  const hour = new Date().getHours()\n  const greeting = hour < 12 ? 'Good morning' : hour < 17 ? 'Good afternoon' : 'Good evening'\n\n  const totalGoals      = metrics?.totalGoals      ?? recentGoals.length\n  const completedGoals  = metrics?.completedGoals  ?? recentGoals.filter(g => g.status === 'COMPLETED').length\n  const inProgressGoals = metrics?.inProgressGoals ?? recentGoals.filter(g => g.status === 'IN_PROGRESS').length\n  const pendingGoals    = metrics?.pendingGoals     ?? recentGoals.filter(g => g.status === 'PENDING').length\n  const completionRate  = metrics?.completionRate   ?? (totalGoals > 0 ? Math.round((completedGoals / totalGoals) * 100) : 0)\n  const pendingReviewsCnt = metrics?.pendingReviews ?? pendingReviews.length\n\n  return (\n    <Layout title=\"My Dashboard\">\n      {/* Welcome */}\n      <div className=\"bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-indigo-600 rounded-2xl p-6 mb-6 text-white\">\n        <h2 className=\"text-2xl font-bold\">{greeting}, {user?.name?.split(' ')[0]}! \ud83d\udc4b</h2>\n        <p className=\"text-blue-100 mt-1\">Here is your personal performance overview.</p>\n        <div className=\"mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-3\">\n          <span ? `${user.department} Department` : 'Employee View'}\n          </span>\n          <span className=\"inline-flex items-center gap-2 bg-white bg-opacity-20 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-sm\">\n            <TrendingUp size={14} />\n            {completionRate}% Completion Rate\n          </span>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {error && (\n        <div className=\"bg-yellow-50 border border-yellow-200 text-yellow-800 rounded-lg px-4 py-3 mb-6 text-sm flex items-center gap-2\">\n          <AlertCircle size={16} /> Dashboard metrics could not be loaded.\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Metrics */}\n      <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6\">\n        <MetricCard title=\"Total Goals\"      value={totalGoals}      icon={Target}      color=\"text-blue-600\"   subtitle=\"All my goals\"         onClick={() => navigate('/goals')} />\n        <MetricCard title=\"Completed\"        value={completedGoals}  icon={CheckCircle} color=\"text-green-600\"  subtitle=\"Successfully finished\" onClick={() => navigate('/goals')} />\n        <MetricCard title=\"In Progress\"      value={inProgressGoals} icon={TrendingUp}  color=\"text-indigo-600\" subtitle=\"Currently working on\"   onClick={() => navigate('/goals')} />\n      </div>\n      <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6\">\n        <MetricCard title=\"Pending Goals\"    value={pendingGoals}    icon={Clock}       color=\"text-yellow-600\" subtitle=\"Awaiting approval\"    onClick={() => navigate('/goals')} />\n        <MetricCard title=\"Completion Rate\"  value={`${completionRate}%`} icon={TrendingUp} color=\"text-purple-600\" subtitle=\"Goals completed\" onClick={() => navigate('/goals')} />\n        <MetricCard title=\"Pending Reviews\"  value={pendingReviewsCnt} icon={ClipboardList} color=\"text-orange-600\" subtitle=\"Awaiting action\" onClick={() => navigate('/reviews')} />\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Two-column */}\n      <div className=\"grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6\">\n        {/* Recent Goals */}\n        <div className=\"card\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center flex items-center gap-1\">\n              View all <ArrowRight size={14} />\n            </button>\n          </div>\n          {recentGoals.length === 0 ? (\n            <div className=\"text-center py-8 text-gray-400\">\n              <Target size={32} className=\"mx-auto mb-2 opacity-50\" />\n              <p className=\"text-sm\">No goals yet</p>\n  ) : (\n            <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n              {recentGoals.slice(0, 5).map(goal => (\n                <div key={goal.goalId}\n                  className=\"flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-100 cursor-pointer transition-colors\"\n                  onClick={() => navigate('/goals')}>\n                  <div className=\"flex-1 min-w-0\">\n                    <p className=\"text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 truncate\">{goal.title}</p>\n                    <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-500 mt-0.5\">{goal.category} \u00b7      <ArrowRight size={16} className=\"text-gray-400 ml-auto\" />\n              </div>\n            )}\n            {pendingReviews.filter(r => r.status === 'PENDING').length > 0 && (\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-blue-50 border border-blue-100 rounded-lg cursor-pointer hover:bg-blue-100 transition-colors\" onClick={() => navigate('/reviews')}>\n                <div className=\"w-8 h-8 bg-blue-100 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center\"><ClipboardList size={16} className=\"text-blue-600\" /></div>\n                <div>\n                  <p </div>\n                <ArrowRight size={16} className=\"text-gray-400 ml-auto\" />\n              </div>\n            )}\n            {pendingReviews.filter(r => r.status === 'MANAGER_REVIEW_COMPLETED').length > 0 && (\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-green-50 border border-green-100 rounded-lg cursor-pointer hover:bg-green-100 transition-colors\" onClick={() => navigate('/reviews')}>\n                <div className=\"w-8 h-8 bg-green-100 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center\"><CheckCircle size={16} className=\"text-green-600\" /></div>\n                <div>\n                  <p className=\"text-sm font-medium text-gray-800\">Review awaiting acknowledgment</p>\n                  <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-500\">Your manager has reviewed your performance</p>\n                </div>\n                <ArrowRight size={16} className=\"text-gray-400 ml-auto\" />\n {/* Filters */}\n      <div className=\"flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 mb-6\">\n        <div className=\"relative flex-1\">\n          <Search size={16} className=\"absolute left-3 top-1/2 toast.error('No manager is assigned to your account.  const handleAddProgress = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await goalService.addProgress(selectedGoal.goalId, progressForm.notes,  const handleSubmitCompletion = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    if (!completionForm.completionNotes) { toast.error('Completion notes are required'); return }\n    setSubmitting(true)\n \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const handleManagerAction = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      switch (actionType) {\n        case 'APPROVE':\n          await goalService.approveGoal(selectedGoal.goalId)\n          toast.success('Goal approved!')\n          break\n        case 'REQUEST_CHANGES':\n          await goalService.requestChanges(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.comments)\n          toast.success('Change request sent to employee')\n          break\n        case 'APPROVE_COMPLETION':\n          await goalService.approveCompletion(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.comments)\n          toast.success('Goal completion approved!')\n          break\n        case 'REJECT_COMPLETION':\n          await goalService.rejectCompletion(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.comments)\n          toast.success('Completion rejected')\n          break\n        case 'REQUEST_EVIDENCE':\n          await goalService.requestAdditionalEvidence(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.message)\n          toast.success('Evidence request sent')\n          break\n        default:\n          break\n      }\n  const handleVerifyEvidence = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await goalService.verifyEvidence(selectedGoal.goalId, evidenceForm.verificationStatus,  const handleDelete = async (goal) => {\n    if (!window.confirm(`Delete goal \"${goal.title}\"? This cannot be undone.`)) return\n    try {\n      await goalService.deleteGoal(goal.goalId)\n      toast.success('Goal deleted')\n      loadGoals()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Failed to delete goal')\n    }\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500 Open manager action modal \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const openAction = (goal, type) => {\n    setSelectedGoal(goal)\n    setActionType(type)\n    setActionForm({ comments: '', message: '' })\n    setShowActionModal(true)\n  }\n\n  // */}\n        <div className=\"relative flex-1 min-w-[200px]\">\n          <Search size={16} className=\"absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400\" />\n          <input\n Renders a single goal with all available actions based on status + role\nfunction GoalCard({ goal, user, isManager, isEmployee, isAdmin, onAddProgress,\n  onSubmitCompletion, onApprove, onRequestChanges, onApproveCompletion,\n  onRejectCompletion, onRequestEvidence, onVerifyEvidence, onDelete }) {\n\n  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false)\n\n  const priorityColors = {\n    CRITICAL: 'border-l-red-500',\n    HIGH: 'border-l-orange-400',\n    MEDIUM: 'border-l-yellow-400',\n    LOW: 'border-l-green-400',\n  }\n\n  const isMyGoal = goal.assignedToUserId === user?.userId\n  const isMyTeamGoal = goal.assignedManagerId === user?.userId\n\n  return (\n    <div className={`card border-l-4 ${priorityColors[goal.priority] || 'border-l-gray-300'} hover:shadow-md transition-shadow`}>\n      {/* Goal Header */}\n      <div className=\"flex items-start justify-between gap-3\">\n        <div className=\"flex-1 min-w-0\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap\">\n            <h3 className=\"font-semibold text-gray-900 truncate\">{goal.title}</h3>\n            <StatusBadge status={goal.status} />\n            <span className=\"text-xs bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full\">\n              {goal.priority}\n            </span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4 mt-1.5 text-xs text-gray-500\">\n            <span>Category: {goal.category}</span>\n            {goal.endDate && <span>Due: {goal.endDate}</span>}\n            {goal.startDate && <span>Started: {goal.startDate}</span>}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Toggle expand */}\n        <button\n          onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}\n          className=\"text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 transition-colors p-1\"\n        >\n          <ChevronDown size={20} className={`transition-transform ${expanded ? 'rotate-180' : ''}`} />\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Expanded Details */}\n      {expanded && (\n        <div className=\"mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-gray-100 space-y-3\">\n          {goal.description && (\n            <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-600\">{goal.description}</p>\n          )}\n          {goal.progressNotes && (\n            <div className=\"bg-blue-50 rounded-lg p-3\">\n              <p className=\"text-xs font-medium text-blue-700 mb-1\">Progress Notes:</p>\n              <p className=\"text-sm text-blue-800\">{goal.progressNotes}</p>\n            </div>\n          )}\n          {goal.completionNotes && (\n            <div className=\"bg-green-50 rounded-lg p-3\">\n              <p className=\"text-xs font-medium text-green-700 mb-1\">Completion Notes:</p>\n              <p className=\"text-sm text-green-800\">{goal.completionNotes}</p>\n            </div>\n          )}\n          {goal.evidenceLink && (\n            <div className=\"bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-3\">\n              <p className=\"text-xs font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1\">Evidence:</p>\n              <a href={goal.evidenceLink} target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"\n                className=\"text-sm text-blue-600 hover:underline break-all\">\n                {goal.evidenceLink}\n              </a>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Action Buttons Row */}\n      <div className=\"flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-3 pt-3 border-t border-gray-100\">\n        {/* \u2500\u2500 EMPLOYEE ACTIONS \u2500\u2500 */}\n        {isEmployee && isMyGoal && (\n          <>\n            {goal.status === 'IN_PROGRESS' && (\n              <button onClick={onAddProgress}\n                className=\"btn-secondary text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                <TrendingUp size={14} /> Update Progress\n              </button>\n            )}\n            {(goal.status === 'IN_PROGRESS') && (\n              <button onClick={onSubmitCompletion}\n                className=\"btn-success text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                <Upload size={14} /> Submit Completion\n              </button>\n            )}\n            {(goal.status === 'PENDING') && (\n              <button onClick={onDelete}\n                className=\"btn-danger text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                <Trash2 size={14} /> Delete\n              </button>\n            )}\n          </>\n        )}\n\n        {/* \u2500\u2500 MANAGER ACTIONS \u2500\u2500 */}\n        {isManager && isMyTeamGoal && (\n          <>\n            {goal.status === 'PENDING' && (\n              <>\n                <button onClick={onApprove}\n                  className=\"btn-success text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                  <CheckCircle size={14} /> Approve\n                </button>\n                <button onClick={onRequestChanges}\n                  className=\"btn-secondary text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                  <MessageSquare size={14} /> Request Changes\n                </button>\n              </>\n            )}\n            {goal.status === 'PENDING_COMPLETION_APPROVAL' && (\n              <>\n                {goal.evidenceLink && (\n                  <button onClick={onVerifyEvidence}\n                    className=\"btn-primary text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                    <Eye size={14} /> Verify Evidence\n                  </button>\n                )}\n                <button onClick={onApproveCompletion}\n                  className=\"btn-success text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                  <CheckCircle size={14} /> Approve\n                </button>\n                <button onClick={onRejectCompletion}\n                  className=\"btn-danger text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                  <XCircle size={14} /> <MessageSquare size={14} /> Request Evidence\n                </button>\n              </>\n            )}\n          </>\n        )}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"

\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Manages the full review workflow:\n//   EMPLOYEE: Submit self-assessment \u2192 Acknowledge manager's review\n//   MANAGER:  Submit manager rating and feedback\n//\n// APIs Used:\n//   GET  /api/v1/performance-reviews\n//   POST /api/v1/performance-reviews         (self-assessment)\n//   PUT  /api/v1/performance-reviews/{id}    (manager review)\n//   PUT  /api/v1/performance-reviews/{id}/draft\n//   POST /api/v1/performance-reviews/{id}/acknowledge\n//   GET  /api/v1/review-cycles/active\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport default function PerformanceReviewsPage() {\n  const { user, isAdmin, isManager, isEmployee } = useAuth()\n\n  const [reviews, setReviews] = useState([])\n  const [activeCycle, setActiveCycle] = useState(null)\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n  const [page, setPage] = useState(0)\n  const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(0)\n\n  // Modals\n  const [showSelfAssessmentModal, setShowSelfAssessmentModal] = useState(false)\n  const [showManagerReviewModal, setShowManagerReviewModal] = useState(false)\n  const [showAcknowledgeModal, setShowAcknowledgeModal] = useState(false)\n  const [showViewModal, setShowViewModal] = useState(false)\n  const [selectedReview, setSelectedReview] = useState(null)\n  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)\n\n  // Self-assessment form state\n  const [selfForm, setSelfForm] = useState({\n    selfAssessment: '',\n    employeeSelfRating: 3,\n  })\n\n  // Manager review form state\n  const [managerForm, setManagerForm] = useState({\n    managerFeedback: '',\n    managerRating: 3,\n    ratingJustification: '',\n    compensationRecommendations: '',\n    nextPeriodGoals: '',\n  })\n\n  // Acknowledge form\n  const [acknowledgeForm, setAcknowledgeForm] = useState({ employeeResponse: '' })\n\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500 Load Data \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  useEffect(() => {\n    loadData()\n  }, [page])\n\n  const loadData = async () => {\n    setLoading(true)\n    try {\n      const [reviewsData, cycleData] = await Promise.allSettled([\n        performanceReviewService.getReviews(page, 10),\n        reviewCycleService.getActiveCycle(),\n      ])\n\n      if (reviewsData.status === 'fulfilled') {\n        const list = reviewsData.value?.content || reviewsData.value || []\n        setReviews(list)\n        setTotalPages(reviewsData.value?.totalPages || 1)\n      }\n      if (cycleData.status === 'fulfilled') {\n        setActiveCycle(cycleData.value?.data || cycleData.value)\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error('Failed to load reviews')\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500 EMPLOYEE: Submit Self-Assessment \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const handleSelfAssessment = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    if (!selfForm.selfAssessment) { toast.error('Self-assessment is required'); return }\n    if (!activeCycle) { toast.error('No active review cycle found'); return }\n\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await performanceReviewService.submitSelfAssessment({\n        cycleId: activeCycle.cycleId,\n        selfAssessment: selfForm.selfAssessment,\n        employeeSelfRating: selfForm.employeeSelfRating,\n      })\n      toast.success('Self-assessment submitted!')\n      setShowSelfAssessmentModal(false)\n      loadData()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Submission failed')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500 MANAGER: Submit Manager Review \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const handleManagerReview = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    if (!managerForm.managerFeedback || !managerForm.ratingJustification) {\n      toast.error('Feedback and justification are required')\n      return\n    }\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await performanceReviewService.submitManagerReview(selectedReview.reviewId, managerForm)\n      toast.success('Manager review submitted!')\n      setShowManagerReviewModal(false)\n      loadData()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Submission failed')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500 EMPLOYEE: Acknowledge Review \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const handleAcknowledge = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await performanceReviewService.acknowledgeReview(\n        selectedReview.reviewId,\n        acknowledgeForm.employeeResponse\n      )\n      toast.success('Review acknowledged!')\n      setShowAcknowledgeModal(false)\n      loadData()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Failed to acknowledge')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500 Star Rating Component \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const StarRating = ({ value, onChange, readOnly = false }) => (\n    <div className=\"flex gap-1\">\n      {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((star) => (\n        <button\n          key={star}\n          type=\"button\"\n          onClick={() => !readOnly && onChange && onChange(star)}\n          className={`text-2xl transition-colors ${\n            star <= value ? 'text-yellow-400' : 'text-gray-200'\n          } ${!readOnly ? 'hover:text-yellow-300 cursor-pointer' : 'cursor-default'}`}\n        >\n          \u2605\n        </button>\n      ))}\n      <span className=\"ml-2 text-sm text-gray-500 self-center\">{value}/5</span>\n    </div>\n  )\n\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500 Render \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  return (\n    <Layout title=\"Performance Reviews\">\n      {/* Active Cycle Banner */}\n      {activeCycle && (\n        <div className=\"bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 rounded-xl p-4 mb-6 flex items-center justify-between\">\n          <div>\n            <p className=\"text-sm font-semibold text-blue-800\">Active Review Cycle</p>\n            <p className=\"text-lg font-bold text-blue-900\">{activeCycle.title}</p>\n            <p className=\"text-xs text-blue-600\">\n              {activeCycle.startDate} \u2192 {activeCycle.endDate}\n            </p>\n          </div>\n          {/* Employee: Submit self-assessment */}\n          {isEmployee() && (\n            <button\n              onClick={() => setShowSelfAssessmentModal(true)}\n              className=\"btn-primary flex items-center gap-2\"\n            >\n              <Send size={16} /> Submit Self-Assessment\n            </button>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* No Active Cycle */}\n      {!activeCycle && !loading && (\n        <div className=\"bg-yellow-50 border border-yellow-200 rounded-xl p-4 mb-6 text-yellow-800 text-sm\">\n          No active review cycle at this time. Contact your administrator.\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Reviews List */}\n      {loading ? (\n        <LoadingSpinner message=\"Loading reviews...\" />\n      ) : reviews.length === 0 ? (\n        <div className=\"card text-center py-16\">\n          <ClipboardList size={48} className=\"mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300\" />\n          <p className=\"text-gray-500 font-medium\">No performance reviews found</p>\n          <p className=\"text-gray-400 text-sm mt-1\">\n            {isEmployee()\n              ? 'Submit your self-assessment during an active review cycle.'\n              : 'Team reviews will appear here once employees submit their self-assessments.'}\n          </p>\n        </div>\n      ) : (\n        <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n          {reviews.map((review) => (\n            <ReviewCard\n              key={review.reviewId}\n              review={review}\n              user={user}\n              isManager={isManager()}\n              isEmployee={isEmployee()}\n              onManagerReview={() => {\n                setSelectedReview(review)\n                setManagerForm({ managerFeedback: '', managerRating: 3, ratingJustification: '', compensationRecommendations: '', nextPeriodGoals: '' })\n                setShowManagerReviewModal(true)\n              }}\n              onAcknowledge={() => {\n                setSelectedReview(review)\n                setAcknowledgeForm({ employeeResponse: '' })\n                setShowAcknowledgeModal(true)\n              }}\n              onView={() => {\n                setSelectedReview(review)\n                setShowViewModal(true)\n              }}\n            />\n          ))}\n          <Pagination currentPage={page} totalPages={totalPages} onPageChange={setPage} />\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550 MODALS \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550 */}\n\n      {/* Self-Assessment Modal (Employee) */}\n      <Modal isOpen={showSelfAssessmentModal} onClose={() => setShowSelfAssessmentModal(false)}\n        title=\"Submit Self-Assessment\" size=\"lg\">\n        <form onSubmit={handleSelfAssessment} className=\"space-y-5\">\n          {activeCycle && (\n            <div className=\"bg-blue-50 rounded-lg p-3 text-sm text-blue-800\">\n              Review Cycle: <strong>{activeCycle.title}</strong>\n            </div>\n          )}\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Self-Assessment *</label>\n            <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-500 mb-2\">\n              Reflect on your performance this cycle. What did you accomplish? What challenges did you face?\n            </p>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" rows={6}\n              value={selfForm.selfAssessment}\n              onChange={e => setSelfForm({ ...selfForm, selfAssessment: e.target.value })}\n              placeholder=\"Describe your achievements, learnings, and areas for growth...\" />\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Self Rating</label>\n            <div className=\"mt-2\">\n              <StarRating\n                value={selfForm.employeeSelfRating}\n                onChange={(v) => setSelfForm({ ...selfForm, employeeSelfRating: v })}\n              />\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-3\">\n            <button type=\"button\" onClick={() => setShowSelfAssessmentModal(false)} className=\"btn-secondary flex-1\">Cancel</button>\n            <button type=\"submit\" disabled={submitting} className=\"btn-primary flex-1\">\n              {submitting ? 'Submitting...' : 'Submit Assessment'}\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </form>\n      </Modal>\n\n      {/* Manager Review Modal */}\n      <Modal isOpen={showManagerReviewModal} onClose={() => setShowManagerReviewModal(false)}\n        title=\"Submit Manager Review\" size=\"lg\">\n        <form onSubmit={handleManagerReview} className=\"space-y-4\">\n          {selectedReview && (\n            <div className=\"bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-3 text-sm\">\n              <p className=\"font-medium\">Employee Self-Assessment:</p>\n              <p className=\"text-gray-600 mt-1\">{selectedReview.selfAssessment || 'Not provided'}</p>\n              <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-400 mt-2\">Self Rating: {selectedReview.employeeSelfRating}/5</p>\n            </div>\n          )}\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Manager Feedback *</label>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" rows={5}\n employee's performance...\" />\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Performance Rating</label>\n            <div className=\"mt-2\">\n              <StarRating\n                value={managerForm.managerRating}\n                onChange={(v) => setManagerForm({ ...managerForm, managerRating: v })}\n              />\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Rating Justification *</label>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" rows={3}\n              value={managerForm.ratingJustification}\n              onChange={e => setManagerForm({ ...managerForm, ratingJustification: e.target.value })}\n              placeholder=\"Explain why you gave this rating...\" />\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Compensation Recommendations</label>\n            <input className=\"input-field\" salary increase, bonus eligible\" />\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Goals for Next Period</label>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" 'Submitting...' : 'Submit Review'}\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </form>\n      </Modal>\n\n      {/* Acknowledge Modal (Employee) */}\n      <Modal isOpen={showAcknowledgeModal} onClose={() => setShowAcknowledgeModal(false)}\n        title=\"Acknowledge Manager Review\">\n        <form onSubmit={handleAcknowledge} className=\"space-y-4\">\n          {selectedReview && (\n            <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n              <div className=\"bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-3 text-sm\">\n                <p className=\"font-medium text-gray-700\">Manager Feedback:</p>\n                <p className=\"text-gray-600 mt-1\">{selectedReview.managerFeedback}</p>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-600\">\n                <Star size={16} className=\"text-yellow-400\" />\n                Manager Rating: <strong>{selectedReview.managerRating}/5</strong>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Your Response (optional)</label>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" rows={4}\n              value={acknowledgeForm.employeeResponse}\n              onChange={e => setAcknowledgeForm({ ...acknowledgeForm, employeeResponse: e.target.value })}\n              placeholder=\"Share any thoughts or comments on this review...\" />\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-lg p-3 text-sm text-green-800\">\n            By acknowledging, you confirm you have read and understood the review.\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-3\">\n            <button type=\"button\" onClick={() => setShowAcknowledgeModal(false)} className=\"btn-secondary flex-1\">Cancel</button>\n            <button type=\"submit\" disabled={submitting} className=\"btn-success flex-1\">\n              {submitting ? className=\"text-xs text-blue-600 mt-2\">Self Rating: {selectedReview.employeeSelfRating}/5</p>\n              </div>\n            )}\n            {selectedReview.managerFeedback && (\n              <div className=\"bg-green-50 rounded-lg p-4\">\n                <p className=\"text-xs font-semibold text-green-700 uppercase mb-2\">Manager Review</p>\n                <p className=\"text-sm </div>\n            )}\n            {selectedReview.employeeResponse && (\n              <div className=\"bg-purple-50 rounded-lg p-4\">\n                <p className=\"text-xs font-semibold <button onClick={() => setShowViewModal(false)} className=\"btn-secondary w-full\">Close</button>\n          </div>\n        )}\n      </Modal>\n    </Layout>\n  )\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 REVIEW CARD COMPONENT ReviewCard({ review, user, isManager, isEmployee, onManagerReview, onAcknowledge, onView }) {\n  const isMyReview = review.userId === user?.userId\n  const isManagerReview = review.reviewedBy === user?.userId\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"card hover:shadow-md transition-shadow\">\n      <div className=\"flex items-start justify-between gap-3\">\n        <div className=\"flex-1\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap\">\n            <StatusBadge status={review.status} />\n            <span className=\"text-sm font-medium text-gray-800\">\n              {isManager ? `User ID: ${review.userId}` : 'My Review'}\n            </span>\n          </div>\n          <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1\">\n            {review.submittedDate ? `Submitted: ${review.submittedDate?.split('T')[0]}` : 'Draft'}\n            {review.managerRating && ` \u00b7 Manager Rating: ${review.managerRating}/5`}\n          </p>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Action buttons */}\n        <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n          <button onClick={onView} className=\"btn-secondary text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n            <Eye size={14} /> View\n          </button>\n          {isManager && review.status === 'SELF_ASSESSMENT_COMPLETED' && (\n            <button onClick={onManagerReview} className=\"btn-primary text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n              <ClipboardList size={14} /> Review\n            </button>\n          )}\n          {isEmployee && isMyReview && review.status === 'MANAGER_REVIEW_COMPLETED' && (\n            <button onClick={onAcknowledge} className=\"btn-success text-xs py-1.5 px-3 flex items-center gap-1\">\n              <CheckCircle size={14} /> Acknowledge\n            </button>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"

'Good morning' : hour < 17 ? 'Good afternoon' : 'Good evening'\n\n  // Derived metric values\n  const totalMembers      = metrics?.teamSize ?? (\n            <div className=\"text-center py-8 text-gray-400\">\n              <Target size={32} className=\"mx-auto mb-2 opacity-50\" />\n              <p className=\"text-sm\">No team goals                       "content": "import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'\nimport { ClipboardList, Eye, Search, RefreshCw, ChevronDown } from 'lucide-react'\nimport Layout from '../../components/layout/Layout'\nimport Modal from '../../components/common/Modal'\nimport LoadingSpinner from '../../components/common/LoadingSpinner'\nimport StatusBadge from '../../components/common/StatusBadge'\nimport Pagination from '../../components/common/Pagination'\nimport { performanceReviewService, reviewCycleService } from '../../services/reviewService'\nimport userService from '../../services/userService'\nimport { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext'\nimport toast from 'react-hot-toast'\n\nfunction MetricChip({ label, value, color }) {\n  return (\n    <div className={`rounded-xl p-4 ${color}`}>\n      <p className=\"text-2xl font-bold\">{value ?? '\u2014'}</p>\n      <p className=\"text-xs font-medium mt-0.5 opacity-80\">{label}</p>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n\nfunction StarRating({ value, onChange }) {\n  return (\n    <div className=\"flex gap-1\">\n      {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map(star => (\n        <button key={star} type=\"button\" onClick={() => onChange && onChange(star)}\n          className={`text-2xl transition-colors cursor-pointer ${star <= value ? 'text-yellow-400' : 'text-gray-200'} hover:text-yellow-300`}>\n          \u2605\n        </button>\n      ))}\n      <span className=\"ml-2 text-sm text-gray-500 self-center\">{value}/5</span>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n\nconst STATUS_FILTERS = [\n  { value: '', label: 'All Statuses' },\n  { value: 'PENDING', label: 'Pending' },\n  { value: 'SELF_ASSESSMENT_COMPLETED', label: 'Self-Assessment Done' },\n  { value: 'MANAGER_REVIEW_COMPLETED', label: 'Manager Reviewed' },\n  { value: 'COMPLETED_AND_ACKNOWLEDGED', label: 'Acknowledged' },\n]\n\nexport default function ManagerReviewsPage() {\n  const { user } = useAuth()\n\n  const [reviews, setReviews]         = useState([])\n  const [cycles, setCycles]           = useState([])       // all available cycles\n  const [selectedCycleId, setSelectedCycleId] = useState(null)\n  const [userMap, setUserMap]         = useState({})       // userId \u2192 user\n  const [teamMemberIds, setTeamMemberIds] = useState(new Set()) // for filtering\n\n  const [loading, setLoading]         = useState(true)\n  const [loadingCycles, setLoadingCycles] = useState(true)\n  const [page, setPage]               = useState(0)\n  const [totalPages, setTotalPages]   = useState(0)\n  const [totalElements, setTotalElements] = useState(0)\n\n  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState('')\n  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm]     = useState('')\n\n  const [selectedReview, setSelectedReview]               = useState(null)\n  const [showReviewModal, setShowReviewModal]             = useState(false)\n  const [showViewModal, setShowViewModal]                 = useState(false)\n  const [submitting, setSubmitting]                       = useState(false)\n  const [managerForm, setManagerForm] = useState({\n    managerFeedback: '', managerRating: 3,\n    ratingJustification: '', compensationRecommendations: '', nextPeriodGoals: '',\n  })\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 Load cycles + team on mount \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  useEffect(() => {\n    loadCycles()\n    if (user?.userId) loadTeam()\n  }, [user?.userId])\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 Load reviews when selected cycle or page changes \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (selectedCycleId != null) loadReviews()\n  }, [selectedCycleId, page])\n\n  const loadCycles = async () => {\n    setLoadingCycles(true)\n    try {\n      const data = await reviewCycleService.getAllCycles()\n      const list = Array.isArray(data) ? data : (data?.content || [])\n      setCycles(list)\n      // Auto-select: active cycle first, otherwise most recent\n      const active = list.find(c => c.status === 'ACTIVE')\n      const first  = list[0]\n      const pick   = active || first\n      if (pick) setSelectedCycleId(pick.cycleId)\n    } catch {\n      // no cycles available \u2014 leave selectedCycleId null\n    } finally {\n      setLoadingCycles(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const loadTeam = async () => {\n    try {\n      const members = await userService.getTeam(user.userId)\n      const list = Array.isArray(members) ? members : (members?.content || [])\n      const map = {}\n      const ids = new Set()\n      list.forEach(m => { map[m.userId] = m; ids.add(m.userId) })\n      setUserMap(map)\n      setTeamMemberIds(ids)\n    } catch { /* silently fail \u2014 show all reviews if team can't load */ }\n  }\n\n  const loadReviews = async () => {\n    setLoading(true)\n    try {\n      // cycleId is required for manager to see team reviews\n      const data = await performanceReviewService.getReviews(0, 200, selectedCycleId)\n      const list = Array.isArray(data) ? data : (data?.content || [])\n      setReviews(list)\n      setTotalPages(data?.totalPages || 1)\n      setTotalElements(data?.totalElements || list.length)\n    } catch {\n      toast.error('Failed to load reviews')\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const getEmployeeName = (review) => {\n    const u = userMap[review.userId]\n    return u?.name || `User #${review.userId}`\n  }\n\n  const getCycleName = (review) =>\n    review.cycle?.title || (selectedCycleId ? `Cycle #${selectedCycleId}` : '\u2014')\n\n  // Client-side filter: only team members (if team loaded), then status + search\n  const filtered = reviews.filter(r => {\n    if (teamMemberIds.size > 0 && !teamMemberIds.has(r.userId)) return false\n    const matchStatus = !statusFilter || r.status === statusFilter\n    const empName = getEmployeeName(r)\n    const matchSearch = !searchTerm ||\n      String(r.userId).includes(searchTerm) ||\n      empName.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase())\n    return matchStatus && matchSearch\n  })\n\n  // Metrics (over current page's filtered reviews)\n  const total     = filtered.length\n  const pending   = filtered.filter(r => r.status === 'PENDING').length\n  const awaitingReview = filtered.filter(r => r.status === 'SELF_ASSESSMENT_COMPLETED').length\n  const done      = filtered.filter(r =>\n    r.status === 'MANAGER_REVIEW_COMPLETED' || r.status === 'COMPLETED_AND_ACKNOWLEDGED'\n  ).length\n  const avgRating = (() => {\n    const rated = filtered.filter(r => r.managerRating)\n    if (!rated.length) return '\u2014'\n    return (rated.reduce((s, r) => s + r.managerRating, 0) / rated.length).toFixed(1)\n  })()\n\n  const handleManagerReview = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    if (!managerForm.managerFeedback || !managerForm.ratingJustification) {\n      toast.error('Feedback and justification are required'); return\n    }\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await performanceReviewService.submitManagerReview(selectedReview.reviewId, managerForm)\n      toast.success('Manager review submitted!')\n      setShowReviewModal(false)\n      loadReviews()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Submission failed')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const selectedCycle = cycles.find(c => c.cycleId === selectedCycleId)\n\n  return (\n    <Layout title=\"Team Performance Reviews\">\n      {/* Metrics */}\n      <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-6\">\n        <MetricChip label=\"Total Reviews\"      value={total}         color=\"bg-blue-50 text-blue-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Pending Self-Assmt\" value={pending}       color=\"bg-gray-50 text-gray-600\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Awaiting My Review\" value={awaitingReview} color=\"bg-yellow-50 text-yellow-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Completed\"          value={done}          color=\"bg-green-50 text-green-700\" />\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Filters row */}\n      <div className=\"flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 mb-6 flex-wrap\">\n        {/* Cycle selector */}\n        <select\n          value={selectedCycleId ?? ''}\n          onChange={e => { setSelectedCycleId(e.target.value ? Number(e.target.value) : null); setPage(0) }}\n          className=\"input-field w-auto\"\n          disabled={loadingCycles}\n        >\n          {loadingCycles\n            ? <option>Loading cycles...</option>\n            : cycles.length === 0\n              ? <option value=\"\">No review cycles</option>\n              : cycles.map(c => (\n                  <option key={c.cycleId} value={c.cycleId}>\n                    {c.title} {c.status === 'ACTIVE' ? '(Active)' : `(${c.status})`}\n                  </option>\n                ))\n          }\n        </select>\n\n        {/* Status filter */}\n        <select\n          value={statusFilter}\n          onChange={e => { setStatusFilter(e.target.value); setPage(0) }}\n          className=\"input-field w-auto\"\n        >\n          {STATUS_FILTERS.map(o => <option key={o.value} value={o.value}>{o.label}</option>)}\n        </select>\n\n        {/* Search */}\n        <div className=\"relative flex-1 min-w-[200px]\">\n          <Search size={16} className=\"absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400\" />\n          <input type=\"text\" placeholder=\"Search by employee name or ID...\"\n            value={searchTerm} onChange={e => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}\n            className=\"input-field pl-9\" />\n        </div>\n\n        <button onClick={loadReviews} className=\"btn-secondary p-2\" title=\"Refresh\">\n          <RefreshCw size={16} />\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Active cycle info */}\n      {selectedCycle && (\n        <div className={`rounded-xl px-4 py-3 mb-6 text-sm flex items-center gap-3\n          ${selectedCycle.status === 'ACTIVE'\n            ? 'bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 text-blue-800'\n            : 'bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-700'}`}>\n          <span className=\"font-semibold\">{selectedCycle.title}</span>\n          <span className=\"text-xs opacity-70\">{selectedCycle.startDate} \u2192 {selectedCycle.endDate}</span>\n          <span className={`text-xs font-medium px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${\n            selectedCycle.status === 'ACTIVE'\n              ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700'\n              : 'bg-gray-200 text-gray-600'\n          }`}>{selectedCycle.status}</span>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {!selectedCycle && !loadingCycles && (\n        <div className=\"bg-yellow-50 border border-yellow-200 rounded-xl p-4 mb-6 text-yellow-800 text-sm\">\n          No review cycles found. Ask your administrator to create a review cycle.\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Table */}\n      {loading ? (\n        <LoadingSpinner message=\"Loading reviews...\" />\n      ) : filtered.length === 0 ? (\n        <div className=\"card text-center py-16\">\n          <ClipboardList size={48} className=\"mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300\" />\n          <p className=\"text-gray-500 font-medium\">No reviews found</p>\n          <p className=\"text-gray-400 text-sm mt-1\">\n            {!selectedCycle ? 'Select a review cycle above.' : 'No reviews match your filters.'}\n          </p>\n        </div>\n      ) : (\n        <div className=\"card p-0 overflow-hidden\">\n          <div {['Employee', 'Cycle', 'Status', 'Self Rating', 'Manager Rating', 'Submitted', 'Actions'].map(h => (\n                    <th key={h} className=\"text-left px-4 py-3 text-xs font-semibold text-gray-600 uppercase tracking-wider whitespace-nowrap\">{h}</th>\n                  ))}\n                </tr>\n              </thead>\n              <tbody className=\"divide-y divide-gray-100\">\n                {filtered.map(review => (\n                  <tr key={review.reviewId} className=\"hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors\">\n                    <td className=\"px-4 py-3\">\n                      <p className=\"font-medium text-gray-800\">{getEmployeeName(review)}</p>\n                      <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-400\">ID: {review.userId}</p>\n                    </td>\n                    <td className=\"px-4 py-3 text-xs text-gray-600 whitespace-nowrap\">\n                      {getCycleName(review)}\n                    </td>\n                    <td className=\"px-4 py-3\"><StatusBadge status={review.status} /></td>\n                    <td className=\"px-4 py-3 text-gray-600\">\n                      {review.employeeSelfRating ? {review.submittedDate?.split('T')[0] || '\u2014'}\n                    </td>\n                    <td className=\"px-4 py-3\">\n                      <div className=\"flex gap-1 flex-wrap\">\n                        <button\n                          onClick={() => { setSelectedReview(review); setShowViewModal(true) }}\n                          className=\"btn-secondary text-xs py-1 px-2 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                          <Eye size={12} /> View\n                        </button>\n                        {review.status === 'SELF_ASSESSMENT_COMPLETED' && (\n                          <button\n                            onClick={() => {\n                              setSelectedReview(review)\n                              setManagerForm({ managerFeedback: '', managerRating: 3, ratingJustification: '', compensationRecommendations: '', nextPeriodGoals: '' })\n                              setShowReviewModal(true)\n                            }}\n          )}\n                      </div>\n                    </td>\n                  </tr>\n                ))}\n              </tbody>\n            </table>\n          </div>\n          <div </div>\n          )}\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Manager Feedback *</label>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" rows={5}\n              value={managerForm.managerFeedback}\n              onChange={e => setManagerForm({ ...managerForm, managerFeedback: e.target.value })}\n              placeholder=\"Provide detailed feedback on this employee's performance...\" />\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Performance Rating</label>\n            <div className=\"mt-2\">\n              <StarRating value={managerForm.managerRating} onChange={v => setManagerForm({ ...managerForm, managerRating: v })} />\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Rating Justification *</label>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" rows={3}\n              value={managerForm.ratingJustification}\n              onChange={e =>
