                      "content": "import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'\nimport {\n  Target, Search, CheckCircle, XCircle, MessageSquare,\n  Eye, ChevronDown, RefreshCw, Filter,\n} from 'lucide-react'\nimport Layout from '../../components/layout/Layout'\nimport LoadingSpinner from '../../components/common/LoadingSpinner'\nimport StatusBadge from '../../components/common/StatusBadge'\nimport Modal from '../../components/common/Modal'\nimport Pagination from '../../components/common/Pagination'\nimport goalService from '../../services/goalService'\nimport userService from '../../services/userService'\nimport { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext'\nimport toast from 'react-hot-toast'\n\nconst STATUS_OPTIONS = [\n  { value: '', label: 'All Statuses' },\n  { value: 'PENDING', label: 'Pending Approval' },\n  { value: 'IN_PROGRESS', label: 'In Progress' },\n  { value: 'PENDING_COMPLETION_APPROVAL', label: 'Pending Completion' },\n  { value: 'COMPLETED', label: 'Completed' },\n  { value: 'REJECTED', label: 'Rejected' },\n]\n\nconst PRIORITY_OPTIONS = ['', 'LOW', 'MEDIUM', 'HIGH', 'CRITICAL']\nconst CATEGORY_OPTIONS = ['', 'TECHNICAL', 'BEHAVIORAL', 'PROFESSIONAL_DEVELOPMENT', 'OTHER']\n\nfunction MetricChip({ label, value, color }) {\n  return (\n    <div className={`rounded-xl p-4 ${color}`}>\n      <p className=\"text-2xl font-bold\">{value ?? '\u2014'}</p>\n      <p className=\"text-xs font-medium mt-0.5 opacity-80\">{label}</p>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n\nexport default function TeamGoalsPage() {\n  const { user } = useAuth()\n  const [goals, setGoals]           = useState([])\n  const [loading, setLoading]       = useState(true)\n  const [page, setPage]             = useState(0)\n  const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(0)\n  const [totalElements, setTotalElements] = useState(0)\n  const [userMap, setUserMap]       = useState({}) // userId -> user object\n\n  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter]     = useState('')\n  const [priorityFilter, setPriorityFilter] = useState('')\n  const [categoryFilter, setCategoryFilter] = useState('')\n  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm]         = useState('')\n\n  const [selectedGoal, setSelectedGoal] = useState(null)\n  const [actionType, setActionType]     = useState('')\n  const [actionForm, setActionForm]     = useState({ comments: '', message: '' })\n  const [showActionModal, setShowActionModal] = useState(false)\n  const [showEvidenceModal, setShowEvidenceModal] = useState(false)\n  const [evidenceForm, setEvidenceForm] = useState({ verificationStatus: 'VERIFIED', notes: '' })\n  const [submitting, setSubmitting]     = useState(false)\n\n  // Load team members for employee name resolution\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (user?.userId) {\n      userService.getTeam(user.userId)\n        .then(members => {\n          const list = Array.isArray(members) ? members : (members?.content || [])\n          const map = {}\n          list.forEach(m => { map[m.userId] = m })\n          setUserMap(map)\n        })\n        .catch(() => {/* silently fail \u2014 names fall back to User #ID */})\n    }\n  }, [user?.userId])\n\n  useEffect(() => { loadGoals() }, [page])\n\n  const loadGoals = async () => {\n    setLoading(true)\n    try {\n      const data = await goalService.getGoals(page, 10)\n      const list = data?.content || data || []\n      setGoals(list)\n      setTotalPages(data?.totalPages || 1)\n      setTotalElements(data?.totalElements || list.length)\n    } catch {\n      toast.error('Failed to load team goals')\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Resolve employee name from userMap or fallback to User #ID\n  const getEmployeeName = (goal) => {\n    if (goal.employeeName) return goal.employeeName\n    const u = userMap[goal.assignedToUserId]\n    return u ? u.name : `User #${goal.assignedToUserId}`\n  }\n\n  // Client-side filters \u2014 status, priority, category, and search all applied here\n  const filtered = goals.filter(g => {\n    const empName = getEmployeeName(g)\n    const matchSearch  = !searchTerm ||\n      g.title?.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||\n      empName.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase())\n    const matchStatus  = !statusFilter || g.status === statusFilter\n    const matchPri     = !priorityFilter || g.priority === priorityFilter\n    const matchCat     = !categoryFilter || g.category === categoryFilter\n    return matchSearch && matchStatus && matchPri && matchCat\n  })\n\n  // Metrics\n  const totalGoals       = totalElements\n  const pendingApprovals = goals.filter(g => g.status === 'PENDING').length\n  const inProgress       = goals.filter(g => g.status === 'IN_PROGRESS').length\n  const completed        = goals.filter(g => g.status === 'COMPLETED').length\n\n  const openAction = (goal, type) => {\n    setSelectedGoal(goal)\n    setActionType(type)\n    setActionForm({ comments: '', message: '' })\n    setShowActionModal(true)\n  }\n\n  const handleManagerAction = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      switch (actionType) {\n        case 'APPROVE':\n          await goalService.approveGoal(selectedGoal.goalId); toast.success('Goal approved!'); break\n        case 'REQUEST_CHANGES':\n          await goalService.requestChanges(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.comments); toast.success('Change request sent'); break\n        case 'APPROVE_COMPLETION':\n          await goalService.approveCompletion(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.comments); toast.success('Completion approved!'); break\n        case 'REJECT_COMPLETION':\n          await goalService.rejectCompletion(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.comments); toast.success('Completion rejected'); break\n        case 'REQUEST_EVIDENCE':\n          await goalService.requestAdditionalEvidence(selectedGoal.goalId, actionForm.message); toast.success('Evidence requested'); break\n        default: break\n      }\n      setShowActionModal(false)\n      loadGoals()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Action failed')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const handleVerifyEvidence = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      await goalService.verifyEvidence(selectedGoal.goalId, evidenceForm.verificationStatus, evidenceForm.notes)\n      toast.success('Evidence verification submitted!')\n      setShowEvidenceModal(false)\n      loadGoals()\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(err.response?.data?.msg || 'Failed to verify evidence')\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const actionTitles = {\n    APPROVE: 'Approve Goal', REQUEST_CHANGES: 'Request Changes',\n    APPROVE_COMPLETION: 'Approve Completion', REJECT_COMPLETION: 'Reject Completion',\n    REQUEST_EVIDENCE: 'Request Additional Evidence',\n  }\n\n  const hasActiveFilters = statusFilter || priorityFilter || categoryFilter || searchTerm\n\n  return (\n    <Layout title=\"Team Goals\">\n      {/* Metrics Row */}\n      <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-6\">\n        <MetricChip label=\"Total Team Goals\"    value={totalGoals}       color=\"bg-blue-50 text-blue-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Pending Approvals\"   value={pendingApprovals} color=\"bg-yellow-50 text-yellow-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"In Progress\"         value={inProgress}       color=\"bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Completed\"           value={completed}        color=\"bg-green-50 text-green-700\" />\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Filters */}\n      <div className=\"flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 mb-3 flex-wrap\">\n        <div className=\"relative flex-1 min-w-[200px]\">\n          <Search size={16} className=\"absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400\" />\n          <input\n            type=\"text\"\n            placeholder=\"Search by title or employee name...\"\n            value={searchTerm}\n            onChange={e => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}\n            className=\"input-field pl-9\"\n          />\n        </div>\n        <select value={statusFilter} onChange={e => setStatusFilter(e.target.value)} className=\"input-field w-auto\">\n          {STATUS_OPTIONS.map(o => <option key={o.value} value={o.value}>{o.label}</option>)}\n        </select>\n        <select value={priorityFilter} onChange={e => setPriorityFilter(e.target.value)} className=\"input-field w-auto\">\n          <option value=\"\">All Priorities</option>\n          {PRIORITY_OPTIONS.filter(Boolean).map(p => <option key={p} value={p}>{p}</option>)}\n        </select>\n        <select value={categoryFilter} onChange={e => setCategoryFilter(e.target.value)} className=\"input-field w-auto\">\n          <option value=\"\">All Categories</option>\n          {CATEGORY_OPTIONS.filter(Boolean).map(c => <option key={c} value={c}>{c}</option>)}\n        </select>\n        {hasActiveFilters && (\n          <button onClick={() => { setStatusFilter(''); setPriorityFilter(''); setCategoryFilter(''); setSearchTerm('') }}\n            className=\"btn-secondary text-xs px-3\">\n            Clear\n          </button>\n        )}\n        <button onClick={loadGoals} className=\"btn-secondary p-2\">\n          <RefreshCw size={16} />\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Active filter chips */}\n      {hasActiveFilters && (\n        <div className=\"flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4 text-xs\">\n          {statusFilter && <span text-orange-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-full\">Priority: {priorityFilter}</span>}\n          {categoryFilter && <span className=\"bg-purple-100 text-purple-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-full\">Category: {categoryFilter}</span>}\n          <span className=\"text-gray-500 self-center\">{filtered.length} result{filtered.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''} on this page</span>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Goals Table */}\n      {loading ? (\n        <LoadingSpinner message=\"Loading team goals...\" />\n      ) : filtered.length === 0 ? (\n        <div className=\"card text-center py-16\">\n          <Target size={48} className=\"mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300\" />\n          <p className=\"text-gray-500 font-medium\">No team goals found</p>\n          <p className=\"text-gray-400 text-sm mt-1\">Try adjusting your filters.</p>\n        </div>\n      ) : (\n        <div className=\"card p-0 overflow-hidden\">\n          <div className=\"overflow-x-auto\">\n            <table className=\"w-full text-sm\">\n              <thead className=\"bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-200\">\n                <tr>\n                  {['ID', 'Employee', 'Title', 'Category', 'Priority', 'Status', 'Start Date', 'Due Date', 'Actions'].map(h => (\n                    <th key={h} className=\"text-left px-4 py-3 text-xs font-semibold text-gray-600 uppercase tracking-wider whitespace-nowrap\">{h}</th>\n                  ))}\n                </tr>\n              </thead>\n              <tbody className=\"divide-y divide-gray-100\">\n                {filtered.map(goal => (\n                  <GoalRow\n                    key={goal.goalId}\n                    goal={goal}\n                    employeeName={getEmployeeName(goal)}\n                    onApprove={() => openAction(goal, 'APPROVE')}\n                    onRequestChanges={() => openAction(goal, 'REQUEST_CHANGES')}\n                    onApproveCompletion={() => openAction(goal, 'APPROVE_COMPLETION')}\n                    onRejectCompletion={() => openAction(goal, 'REJECT_COMPLETION')}\n                    onRequestEvidence={() => openAction(goal, 'REQUEST_EVIDENCE')}\n                    onVerifyEvidence={() => { setSelectedGoal(goal); setShowEvidenceModal(true) }}\n                  />\n                ))}\n              </tbody>\n            </table>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"px-4\">\n            <Pagination currentPage={page} totalPages={totalPages} totalElements={totalElements} onPageChange={setPage} />\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Manager Action Modal */}\n      <Modal isOpen={showActionModal} onClose={() => setShowActionModal(false)} title={actionTitles[actionType] || 'Action'}>\n        <form onSubmit={handleManagerAction} className=\"space-y-4\">\n          <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-600 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-3\">Goal: <strong>{selectedGoal?.title}</strong></p>\n          {actionType === 'APPROVE' ? value={evidenceForm.verificationStatus}\n              onChange={e => setEvidenceForm({ ...evidenceForm, verificationStatus: e.target.value })}>\n              <option value=\"VERIFIED\">Verified \u2014 Evidence is acceptable</option>\n              <option value=\"NEEDS_REVISION\">Needs Revision \u2014 More work needed</option>\n              <option value=\"REJECTED\">Rejected \u2014 Does not meet requirements</option>\n            </select>\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"form-label\">Notes</label>\n            <textarea className=\"input-field\" rows={3} value={evidenceForm.notes}\n              onChange={e => setEvidenceForm({ ...evidenceForm, notes: e.target.value })}\n              placeholder=\"Add notes about your verification...\" />\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-3\">\n            <button type=\"button\" onClick={() => setShowEvidenceModal(false)} className=\"btn-secondary flex-1\">Cancel</button>\n            <button type=\"submit\" disabled={submitting} className=\"btn-primary flex-1\">\n              {submitting ? 'Submitting...' : 'Submit Verification'}\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </form>\n      </Modal>\n    </Layout>\n  )\n}\n\nfunction GoalRow({ goal, employeeName, onApprove, onRequestChanges, onApproveCompletion, onRejectCompletion, onRequestEvidence, onVerifyEvidence }) {\n  const priorityColors = { CRITICAL: 'text-red-600 font-bold', HIGH: 'text-orange-500', MEDIUM: 'text-yellow-600', LOW: 'text-green-600' }\n\n  return (\n    <tr className=\"hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors\">\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3 text-xs text-gray-400 font-mono\">#{goal.goalId}</td>\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3 whitespace-nowrap\">\n        <p className=\"text-gray-800 font-medium\">{employeeName}</p>\n        <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-400\">ID: {goal.assignedToUserId}</p>\n      </td>\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3 text-gray-700 max-w-xs\">\n        <p className=\"truncate font-medium\" title={goal.title}>{goal.title}</p>\n        {goal.description && <p className=\"text-xs text-gray-400 truncate mt-0.5\" title={goal.description}>{goal.description}</p>}\n      </td>\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3 text-xs\">\n        <span className=\"bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full\">{goal.category}</span>\n      </td>\n      <td className={`px-4 py-3 text-xs font-semibold ${priorityColors[goal.priority] || 'text-gray-600'}`}>{goal.priority}</td>\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3\"><StatusBadge status={goal.status} /></td>\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3 text-xs text-gray-500 whitespace-nowrap\">{goal.startDate || '\u2014'}</td>\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3 text-xs text-gray-500 whitespace-nowrap\">{goal.endDate || '\u2014'}</td>\n      <td className=\"px-4 py-3\">\n        <div className=\"flex flex-wrap gap-1 min-w-[120px]\">\n          {goal.status === 'PENDING' && (\n            <>\n              <button onClick={onApprove} className=\"btn-success text-xs py-1 px-2 flex items-center gap-1\"><CheckCircle size={12} /> Approve</button>\n              <button onClick={onRequestChanges} className=\"btn-secondary text-xs py-1 px-2 flex items-center gap-1\"><MessageSquare size={12} /> Changes</button>\n            </>\n          )}\n          {goal.status === 'PENDING_COMPLETION_APPROVAL' && (\n            <>\n              {goal.evidenceLink && <button onClick={onVerifyEvidence} className=\"btn-primary text-xs py-1 px-2 flex items-center gap-1\"><Eye size={12} /> Verify</button>}\n              <button onClick={onApproveCompletion} className=\"btn-success text-xs py-1 px-2 flex items-center gap-1\"><CheckCircle size={12} /> Approve</button>\n              <button onClick={onRejectCompletion} className=\"btn-danger text-xs py-1 px-2 flex items-center gap-1\"><XCircle size={12} /> Reject</button>\n              <button onClick={onRequestEvidence} className=\"btn-secondary text-xs py-1 px-2 flex items-center gap-1\"><MessageSquare size={12} /> Evidence</button>\n            </>\n          )}\n          {(goal.status === 'COMPLETED' || goal.status === 'IN_PROGRESS' || goal.status === 'REJECTED') && (\n            <span className=\"text-xs text-gray-400 italic\">No action needed</span>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </td>\n    </tr>\n  )\n}\n"

'\u2014'}</p>\n      <p className=\"text-xs font-medium mt-0.5 opacity-80\">{label}</p>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n\nfunction Avatar({ name, size = 'md' }) {\n  const sizeClass = size === 'lg' ? 'w-14 h-14 text-xl' : 'w-9 h-9 text-sm'\n  return (\n    <div className={`${sizeClass} bg-purple-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-white font-semibold flex-shrink-0`}>\n      {name?.charAt(0)?.toUpperCase() || 'U'}\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n\nexport default function TeamMembersPage() {\n  const { user } = useAuth()\n\n  const [members, setMembers]     = useState([])\n  const [loading, setLoading]     = useState(true)\n  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('')\n  const [deptFilter, setDeptFilter] = useState('')\n\n  const [selectedMember, setSelectedMember] = useState(null)\n  const [memberGoals, setMemberGoals]       = useState([])\n  const [memberReviews, setMemberReviews]   = useState([])\n  const [detailLoading, setDetailLoading]   = useState(false)\n  const [showDetailModal, setShowDetailModal] = useState(false)\n\n  useEffect(() => { loadTeam() }, [])\n\n  const loadTeam = async () => {\n    setLoading(true)\n    try {\n      const data = await userService.getTeam(user.userId)\n      const list = data?.content || data || []\n      setMembers(Array.isArray(list) ? list : [])\n    } catch {\n      // fallback: try getAllUsers and filter\n      try {\n        const data = await userService.getAllUsers(0, 100)\n        const list = data?.content || data || []\n        setMembers(list.filter(u => u.role === 'EMPLOYEE'))\n      } catch {\n        toast.error('Failed to load team members')\n      }\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const openDetail = async (member) => {\n    setSelectedMember(member)\n    setShowDetailModal(true)\n    setDetailLoading(true)\n    try {\n      const [goalsRes, reviewsRes] = await Promise.allSettled([\n        goalService.getGoals(0, 50),\n        performanceReviewService.getReviews(0, 20),\n      ])\n      if (goalsRes.status === 'fulfilled') {\n        const all = goalsRes.value?.content || goalsRes.value || []\n        setMemberGoals(all.filter(g => g.assignedToUserId === member.userId || g.userId === member.userId))\n      }\n      if (reviewsRes.status === 'fulfilled') {\n        const all = reviewsRes.value?.content || reviewsRes.value || []\n        setMemberReviews(all.filter(r => r.userId === member.userId))\n      }\n    } catch {\n      // silently fail\n    } finally {\n      setDetailLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const departments = [...new Set(members.map(m => m.department).filter(Boolean))]\n\n  const filtered = members.filter(m => {\n    const matchSearch = !searchTerm ||\n      m.name?.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||\n      m.email?.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase())\n    const matchDept = !deptFilter || m.department === deptFilter\n    return matchSearch && matchDept\n  })\n\n  // Metrics\n  const activeMembers   = members.filter(m => m.status === 'ACTIVE' || !m.status).length\n  const departments_cnt = [...new Set(members.map(m => m.department).filter(Boolean))].length\n\n  return (\n    <Layout title=\"Team Members\">\n      {/* Metrics */}\n      <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-6\">\n        <MetricChip label=\"Total Members\"   value={members.length}  color=\"bg-purple-50 text-purple-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Active Members\"  value={activeMembers}   color=\"bg-green-50 text-green-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Departments\"     value={departments_cnt} color=\"bg-blue-50 text-blue-700\" />\n        <MetricChip label=\"Inactive\"        value={members.length - activeMembers} color=\"bg-gray-50 text-gray-600\" />\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Filters */}\n      <div className=\"flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 mb-6\">\n        <div className=\"relative flex-1\">\n          <Search size={16} className=\"absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400\" />\n          <input type=\"text\" placeholder=\"Search by name or email...\"\n            value={searchTerm} onChange={e => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}\n            className=\"input-field pl-9\" />\n        </div>\n        {departments.length > 0 && (\n          <select value={deptFilter} onChange={e => setDeptFilter(e.target.value)} className=\"input-field w-auto\">\n            <option value=\"\">All Departments</option>\n            {departments.map(d => <option key={d}>{d}</option>)}\n          </select>\n        )}\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Member Cards Grid */}\n      {loading ? (\n        <LoadingSpinner message=\"Loading team members...\" />\n      ) : filtered.length === 0 ? (\n        <div className=\"card text-center py-16\">\n          <Users size={48} className=\"mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300\" />\n          <p className=\"text-gray-500 font-medium\">No team members found</p>\n          <p className=\"text-gray-400 text-sm mt-1\">Try adjusting your search or filters.</p>\n        </div>\n      ) : (\n        <div className=\"grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4\">\n          {filtered.map(member => (\n            <div\n              key={member.userId}\n              className=\"card hover:shadow-md transition-all cursor-pointer border-l-4 border-l-purple-400\"\n              onClick={() => openDetail(member)}\n            >\n              <div className=\"flex items-start gap-3\">\n                <Avatar name={member.name} />\n                <div className=\"flex-1 min-w-0\">\n                  <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between gap-2\">\n                    <h3 className=\"font-semibold text-gray-900 truncate\">{member.name}</h3>\n                    <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium flex-shrink-0\n                      ${member.status === 'ACTIVE' || !member.status ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-500'}`}>\n                      {member.status || 'ACTIVE'}\n                    </span>\n                  </div>\n                  <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1 mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500\">\n                    <Mail size={12} />\n                    <span className=\"truncate\">{member.email}</span>\n                  </div>\n                  {member.department && (\n                    <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1 mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500\">\n                      <Briefcase size={12} />\n                      <span>{member.department}</span>\n                    </div>\n                  )}\n                </div>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"mt-3 pt-3 border-t border-gray-100 flex items-center justify-between\">\n                <span className=\"text-xs text-gray-400\">ID: {member.userId}</span>\n                <button className=\"text-xs text-purple-600 hover:text-purple-800 flex items-center gap-1\">\n                  <Eye size={12} /> View Details\n                </button>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Member Detail Modal */}\n      <Modal isOpen={showDetailModal} onClose={() => setShowDetailModal(false)} title=\"Team Member Details\" size=\"lg\">\n        {selectedMember && (\n          <div className=\"space-y-5\">\n            {/* Profile Header */}\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4 p-4 bg-purple-50 rounded-xl\">\n              <Avatar name={selectedMember.name} size=\"lg\" />\n              <div>\n                <h3 className=\"text-xl font-bold text-gray-900\">{selectedMember.name}</h3>\n                <p className=\"text-sm [\n        { name: 'Avg Self Rating',    value: +(perfSummary?.avgSelfRating || 0).toFixed(2) },\n        { name: 'Avg Manager Rating', value: +(perfSummary?.avgManagerRating || 0).toFixed(2) },\n      ]\n    : []\n\n  const tabs = [\n    { id: 'overview',     label: 'Overview' },\n    { id: 'goals',        label: 'Goal Analytics' },\n    { id: 'performance',  label: 'Performance' },\n  ]\n\n  if (loading) return <Layout title=\"Team Reports\"><LoadingSpinner message=\"Loading team reports...\" /></Layout>\n\n  const completionRate = dashboard?.totalGoals\n    ? Math.round((dashboard.completedGoals / dashboard.totalGoals) * 100)\n    : null\n\n  return (\n    <Layout title=\"Team Reports\">\n      {/* Generate Buttons */}\n      <div className=\"flex gap-3 mb-6 flex-wrap\">\n        {['TEAM', 'DEPARTMENT'].map(scope => (\n          <button key={scope} onClick={() => handleGenerateReport(scope)}\n            disabled={generating}\n            className=\"btn-secondary flex items-center gap-2 text-sm\">\n            <Download size={16} />\n            {generating ? 'Generating...' : `Generate ${scope} Report`}\n          </button>\n        ))}\n        <button onClick={loadAll} className=\"btn-secondary p-2 ml-auto\"><RefreshCw size={16} /></button>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Tabs */}\n      <div className=\"flex gap-1 bg-gray-100 p-1 rounded-xl mb-6 w-fit\">\n        {tabs.map(tab => (\n          <button key={tab.id} onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.id)}\n            className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-colors ${\n              activeTab === tab.id ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-purple-600' : 'text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-800'\n            }`}>\n            {tab.label}\n          </button>\n        ))}\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Overview Tab */}\n      {activeTab === 'overview' && (\n        <div className=\"space-y-6\">\n          <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4\">\n            <KpiCard label=\"Total Team Goals\"   value={dashboard?.totalGoals ?? dashboard?.totalTeamGoals} icon={Target}    color=\"text-blue-600 bg-blue-50\" />\n            <KpiCard label=\"Completed Goals\"    value={dashboard?.completedGoals}                          icon={Award}     color=\"text-green-600 bg-green-50\" />\n            <KpiCard label=\"Team Size\"          value={dashboard?.teamSize}                                icon={Users}     color=\"text-purple-600 bg-purple-50\" />\n            <KpiCard label=\"Completion Rate\"    value={completionRate != null ? `${completionRate}%` : '\u2014'} icon={TrendingUp} color=\"text-orange-600 bg-orange-50\" />\n          </div>\n\n          {goalStatusData.length > 0 && (\n            <div className=\"card\">\n              <h3 className=\"section-title mb-4\">Goal Status Distribution</h3>\n              <ResponsiveContainer width=\"100%\" height={280}>\n                <PieChart>\n                  <Pie data={goalStatusData} dataKey=\"value\" nameKey=\"name\"\n                    cx=\"50%\" cy=\"50%\" outerRadius={100}\n                    label={({ name, percent }) => `${name} ${(percent * 100).toFixed(0)}%`}>\n                    {goalStatusData.map((_, i) => <Cell key={i} fill={COLORS[i % COLORS.length]} />)}\n                  </Pie>\n                  <Tooltip />\n                </PieChart>\n              </ResponsiveContainer>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Goal Analytics Tab */}\n      {activeTab === 'goals' && (\n        <div className=\"space-y-6\">\n          <div className=\"card\">\n            <h3 className=\"section-title mb-4\">Goal Status Breakdown</h3>\n            {goalStatusData.length > 0 ?     <p>No goal data available yet</p>\n              </div>\n            )}\n          </div>\n\n          {goalAnalytics?.categoryBreakdown && (\n            <div className=\"card\">\n data={Object.entries(goalAnalytics.categoryBreakdown).map(([name, value]) => ({ name, value }))}\n                    dataKey=\"value\" nameKey=\"name\" cx=\"50%\" cy=\"50%\" outerRadius={90}\n                   "content": "import axios from 'axios'\n\n// Base API URL \u2014 all requests go through the Spring Cloud API Gateway (port 8092)\n// The Vite dev server proxies /api \u2192 http://localhost:8092\nconst BASE_URL = '/api/v1'\n\n// Create an Axios instance with default settings\nconst api = axios.create({\n  baseURL: BASE_URL,\n  headers: {\n    'Content-Type': 'application/json',\n  },\n})\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 REQUEST INTERCEPTOR \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Automatically attach the JWT token to every outgoing request\napi.interceptors.request.use(\n  (config) => {\n    // Get the JWT token from localStorage (saved after login)\n    const token = localStorage.getItem('token')\n    if (token) {\n      config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`\n    }\n    return config\n  },\n  (error) => Promise.reject(error)\n)\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 RESPONSE INTERCEPTOR \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// 1. Auto-unwrap the backend's ApiResponse<T> envelope so every service gets\n//    the inner `data` field directly instead of { status, msg, data }.\n// 2. Redirect to /login on 401 Unauthorized.\napi.interceptors.response.use(\n  (response) => {\n    // Every backend endpoint returns ApiResponse<T> = { status, msg, data }\n    // Unwrap it so callers receive T directly via response.data\n    const body = response.data\n    if (\n      body !== null &&\n      typeof body === 'object' &&\n      typeof body.status === 'string' &&\n      'data' in body &&\n      typeof body.msg === 'string'\n    ) {\n      return { ...response, data: body.data }\n    }\n    return response\n  },\n  (error) => {\n    if (error.response?.status === 401) {\n      // Token expired or invalid \u2014 clear storage and redirect to login\n      localStorage.removeItem('token')\n      localStorage.removeItem('user')\n      window.location.href = '/login'\n    }\n    return Promise.reject(error)\n  }\n)\n\nexport default api\n"

api.put(`/goals/${goalId}`, {\n      title: goalData.title,\n      desc: goalData.description,\n      cat: goalData.category,\n      pri: goalData.priority,\n      startDt: goalData.startDate || null,\n      endDt: goalData.endDate || null,\n      mgrId: goalData.assignedManagerId ? parseInt(goalData.assignedManagerId) : null,\n    })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * DELETE */\n  requestChanges: async (goalId, comments) => {\n    const response = await api.put(`/goals/${goalId}/request-changes`, { comments })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * POST                   "content": "import api from './api'\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 NOTIFICATION SERVICE \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nconst response = await api.get('/notifications', { params: { page, size } })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * PUT /api/v1/notifications/{notifId}\n   * Mark a single notification as read.\n   */\n  markAsRead: async (notifId) => {\n    const response = await api.put(`/notifications/${notifId}`)\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * PUT /api/v1/notifications/mark-all-read\n   * Mark ALL notifications as read.\n   */\n  markAllAsRead: async () => {\n    const response = await api.put('/notifications/mark-all-read')\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Create an SSE EventSource connection for real-time notifications.\n   * GET /api/v1/notifications/stream\n   *\n   * SSE = Server-Sent Events: the server pushes data to the client in real-time\n   * without the client having to poll repeatedly.\n   *\n   * @param {Function} onMessage - Callback when a new notification arrives\n   * @param {Function} onError - Callback when connection error occurs\n   * @returns {EventSource} - The EventSource object (call .close() to disconnect)\n   */\n  subscribeToStream: (onMessage, onError) => {\n    const token = localStorage.getItem('token')\n    // SSE requires the token in the URL as EventSource doesn't support custom headers\n    const url = `/api/v1/notifications/stream?token=${token}`\n\n    const eventSource = new EventSource(url)\n\n    eventSource.onmessage = (event) => {\n      try {\n        const notification = JSON.parse(event.data)\n        onMessage(notification)\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Failed to parse SSE notification:', err)\n      }\n    }\n\n    eventSource.onerror = (err) => {\n      console.error('SSE connection error:', err)\n      if (onError) onError(err)\n    }\n\n    return eventSource\n  },\n}\n\nexport default notificationService\n"

const reviewCycleService = {\n  /**\n   * GET /api/v1/review-cycles\n   * Get all review cycles.\n   */\n  getAllCycles: async () => {\n    const response = await api.get('/review-cycles')\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * GET /api/v1/review-cycles/active\n   * Get the currently active review cycle.\n   */\n  getActiveCycle: async () => {\n    const response = await api.get('/review-cycles/active')\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * GET /api/v1/review-cycles/{cycleId}\n   * Get a specific review cycle by ID.\n   */\n  getCycleById: async (cycleId) => {\n    const response = await api.get(`/review-cycles/${cycleId}`)\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * POST /api/v1/review-cycles\n   * Create a new review cycle (ADMIN only).\n   * Backend CreateReviewCycleRequest fields: title, startDt, endDt, status, reqCompAppr, evReq\n   */\n  createCycle: async (cycleData) => {\n    const response = await api.post('/review-cycles', {\n      title: cycleData.title,\n      startDt: cycleData.startDate,\n      endDt: cycleData.endDate,\n      status: 'UPCOMING',\n      reqCompAppr: cycleData.requiresCompletionApproval,\n      evReq: cycleData.evidenceRequired,\n    })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * PUT /api/v1/review-cycles/{cycleId}\n   * Update a review cycle (ADMIN only).\n   * Backend CreateReviewCycleRequest fields: title, startDt, endDt, status, reqCompAppr, evReq\n   * existingStatus: the current status of the cycle (preserved on update)\n   */\n  updateCycle: async (cycleId, cycleData, existingStatus = 'UPCOMING') => {\n    const response = await api.put(`/review-cycles/${cycleId}`, {\n      title: cycleData.title,\n      startDt: cycleData.startDate,\n      endDt: cycleData.endDate,\n      status: existingStatus,\n      reqCompAppr: cycleData.requiresCompletionApproval,\n      evReq: cycleData.evidenceRequired,\n    })\n    return response.data\n  },\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Performance Reviews const performanceReviewService = {\n  /**\n   * GET /api/v1/performance-reviews\n   * Get all performance reviews (filtered by role).\n   * Employee: their own reviews\n   * Manager: reviews for their team\n   * Admin: all reviews\n   */\n  getReviews: async (page = 0, size = 10, cycleId = null) => {\n    const params = { page, size }\n    if (cycleId) params.cycleId = cycleId\n    const response = await api.get('/performance-reviews', { params })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * GET /api/v1/performance-reviews/{reviewId}\n   * Get a specific review by ID.\n   */\n  getReviewById: async (reviewId) => {\n    const response = await api.get(`/performance-reviews/${reviewId}`)\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * POST /api/v1/performance-reviews\n   * Employee submits their self-assessment.\n   * Backend SelfAssessmentRequest fields: cycleId, selfAssmt, selfRating\n   */\n  submitSelfAssessment: async (assessmentData) => {\n    const response = await api.post('/performance-reviews', {\n      cycleId: assessmentData.cycleId,\n      selfAssmt: assessmentData.selfAssessment,\n      selfRating: assessmentData.employeeSelfRating,\n    })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * PUT /api/v1/performance-reviews/{reviewId}/draft\n   * Save a draft self-assessment (Employee).\n   */\n  saveDraft: async (reviewId, draftData) => {\n    const response = await api.put(`/performance-reviews/${reviewId}/draft`, draftData)\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * PUT /api/v1/performance-reviews/{reviewId}\n   * Manager submits their review and rating for an employee.\n   * Backend ManagerReviewRequest fields: mgrFb, mgrRating, ratingJust, compRec, nextGoals\n   */\n  submitManagerReview: async (reviewId, reviewData) => {\n    const response = await api.put(`/performance-reviews/${reviewId}`, {\n      mgrFb: reviewData.managerFeedback,\n      mgrRating: reviewData.managerRating,\n      ratingJust: reviewData.ratingJustification,\n      compRec: reviewData.compensationRecommendations,\n      nextGoals: reviewData.nextPeriodGoals,\n    })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * POST /api/v1/performance-reviews/{reviewId}/acknowledge\n   * Employee acknowledges they have read the manager's review.\n   * Backend reads body.get(\"response\")\n   */\n  acknowledgeReview: async (reviewId, employeeResponse) => {\n    const response = await api.post(`/performance-reviews/${reviewId}/acknowledge`, {\n      response: employeeResponse,\n    })\n    return response.data\n Supports pagination.\n   */\n  getAllUsers: async (page = 0, size = 20) => {\n    const response = await api.get('/users', { params: { page, size } })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * GET /api/v1/users/{userId}\n   * Get a specific user by their ID.\n   */\n  getUserById: async (userId) => {\n    const response = await api.get(`/users/${userId}`)\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * POST /api/v1/users\n   * Create a new user (ADMIN only).\n   * Backend CreateUserRequest fields: name, email, password, role, dept, mgrId, status\n   */\n  createUser: async (userData) => {\n    const response = await api.post('/users', {\n      name: userData.name,\n      email: userData.email,\n      password: userData.password,\n      role: userData.role,\n      dept: userData.department,\n      mgrId: userData.managerId ? parseInt(userData.managerId) : null,\n      status: userData.status || 'ACTIVE',\n    })\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * PUT /api/v1/users/{userId}\n   * Update an existing user (ADMIN only).\n   * Backend CreateUserRequest fields: name, email, password, role, dept, mgrId, status\n   */\n  updateUser: async (userId, userData) => {\n    const body = {\n      name: userData.name,\n      email: userData.email,\n      role: userData.role,\n      dept: userData.department,\n      mgrId: userData.managerId ? parseInt(userData.managerId) : null,\n      status: userData.status || 'ACTIVE',\n    }\n    if (userData.password) body.password = userData.password\n    const response = await api.put(`/users/${userId}`, body)\n    return response.data\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * GET /api/v1/users/{userId}/team\n   * Get all team members under a manager (MANAGER role).\n   */\n  getTeam: async (userId) => {\n    const response = await api.get(`/users/${userId}/team`)\n    return response.data\n  },\n}\n\nexport default userService\n"
